 			if(document.getElementById('btn-google-signin3-header-right')){
 				self.googleAttachSignin(document.getElementById('btn-google-signin3-header-right'));

 			// Sign the user in, and then retrieve their ID.

 		// 	'scope': 'profile email',
 		// 	'width': 50,

 		// 	'longtitle': false,
 		// 	'theme': 'dark',
 		// 	'onsuccess': onGoogleSignIn,
 		// 	'onfailure': onGoogleFailure
 		// });
 	};
 
 	self.googleAttachSignin = function(element) {
 		google_auth2.attachClickHandler(element, {}, self.onGoogleSignIn, self.onGoogleFailure);
 	};
 
 	self.onGoogleSignIn = function(googleUser) {
 		// Useful data for your client-side scripts:
 		// var profile = googleUser.getBasicProfile();
 		// console.log("ID: " + profile.getId()); // Don't send this directly to your server!
 		// console.log('Full Name: ' + profile.getName());
 		// console.log('Given Name: ' + profile.getGivenName());
 		// console.log('Family Name: ' + profile.getFamilyName());
 		// console.log("Image URL: " + profile.getImageUrl());
 		// console.log("Email: " + profile.getEmail());
 		self.googleSignOnWithBackend(googleUser);
 	};
 
 	self.onGoogleFailure = function(error){
 		//console.log('onFailure:');
 		//console.log(arguments);
 		//alert(JSON.stringify(error, undefined, 2));
 	};
 
 	self.googleSignOnWithBackend = function(user){
 		var user = gapi.auth2.getAuthInstance().currentUser.get();
 		var profile = user.getBasicProfile();
 		var id_token = user.getAuthResponse().id_token;
 
 		if(id_token === undefined) return;
 
 		// $.post('plugin/?id=google:verify&action=tryLogin', {id_token: id_token}, function(data){
 		// 	console.log(data);
 		// }, 'json');
 		var form = $('<form action="plugin/?id=google:verify&action=tryLogin&referer=" method="post"></form>');
 		form.append('<input type="hidden" name="id_token" value="">');
 		form.append('<input type="hidden" name="regsubmit" value="yes">');
 		form.append('<input type="hidden" name="formhash" value="07b03726">');
 		form.append('<input type="hidden" name="referer" id="referer" value="" />');
 		form.find('input[name="id_token"]').val(id_token);
 		jQuery.post('plugin/?id=google:verify&action=tryLogin&referer=',jQuery(form[0]).serialize(),function(data){
 			window.location.href='https://www.jkforum.net/member.php?mod=logging&action=login&mobile=yes&g=return';
 		});
 	};
 
 	self.on = function(eventName, func){
 		self[eventName] && self[eventName].push(func);
 	};
 	self.dispatchEvent = function(eventName, event, context){
 		for(var i in self[eventName]){
 			self[eventName][i].call(context, event);
 		}
 	};
 })).$new(jQuery));
 
 function JK_GAPI_LOADED(){
 	jkfjs.google.onLoadGAPI.apply(this, arguments);
 }

 			});
 
 			self.googleAttachSignin(document.getElementById('btn-google-signin2-header-right'));
 			if(document.getElementById('btn-google-signin3-header-right')){
 				self.googleAttachSignin(document.getElementById('btn-google-signin3-header-right'));
 			}
 
 			// Sign the user in, and then retrieve their ID.
 			// auth2.signIn().then(function() {
 			// console.log(auth2.currentUser.get().getId());
 			// });
 		});

 		// 	'scope': 'profile email',
 		// 	'width': 50,
 		// 	'height': 50,
 		// 	'longtitle': false,
 		// 	'theme': 'dark',
 		// 	'onsuccess': onGoogleSignIn,
 		// 	'onfailure': onGoogleFailure
 		// });
 	};
 
 	self.googleAttachSignin = function(element) {
 		google_auth2.attachClickHandler(element, {}, self.onGoogleSignIn, self.onGoogleFailure);
 	};
 
 	self.onGoogleSignIn = function(googleUser) {
 		// Useful data for your client-side scripts:
 		// var profile = googleUser.getBasicProfile();
 		// console.log("ID: " + profile.getId()); // Don't send this directly to your server!
 		// console.log('Full Name: ' + profile.getName());
 		// console.log('Given Name: ' + profile.getGivenName());
 		// console.log('Family Name: ' + profile.getFamilyName());
 		// console.log("Image URL: " + profile.getImageUrl());
 		// console.log("Email: " + profile.getEmail());
 		self.googleSignOnWithBackend(googleUser);
 	};
 
 	self.onGoogleFailure = function(error){
 		//console.log('onFailure:');
 		//console.log(arguments);
 		//alert(JSON.stringify(error, undefined, 2));
 	};
 
 	self.googleSignOnWithBackend = function(user){
 		var user = gapi.auth2.getAuthInstance().currentUser.get();
 		var profile = user.getBasicProfile();
 		var id_token = user.getAuthResponse().id_token;
 
 		if(id_token === undefined) return;
 
 		// $.post('plugin/?id=google:verify&action=tryLogin', {id_token: id_token}, function(data){
 		// 	console.log(data);
 		// }, 'json');
 		var form = $('<form action="plugin/?id=google:verify&action=tryLogin&referer=" method="post"></form>');
 		form.append('<input type="hidden" name="id_token" value="">');
 		form.append('<input type="hidden" name="regsubmit" value="yes">');
 		form.append('<input type="hidden" name="formhash" value="07b03726">');
 		form.append('<input type="hidden" name="referer" id="referer" value="" />');
 		form.find('input[name="id_token"]').val(id_token);
 		jQuery.post('plugin/?id=google:verify&action=tryLogin&referer=',jQuery(form[0]).serialize(),function(data){
 			window.location.href='https://www.jkforum.net/member.php?mod=logging&action=login&mobile=yes&g=return';
 		});
 	};
 
 	self.on = function(eventName, func){
 		self[eventName] && self[eventName].push(func);
 	};
 	self.dispatchEvent = function(eventName, event, context){
 		for(var i in self[eventName]){
 			self[eventName][i].call(context, event);
 		}
 	};
 })).$new(jQuery));
 
 function JK_GAPI_LOADED(){
 	jkfjs.google.onLoadGAPI.apply(this, arguments);
 }

    jkfjs.install('google', (new JKDefineClass('GooglePlugin', function($){
 	var self = this;
 	var google_auth2;
 
 	self.onLoadGAPI = function(){
 		gapi.load('auth2', function() {
 			google_auth2 = gapi.auth2.init({
 				client_id: "822113201045-d7i1ef7c3djluutebumk2l4n8aa6if3s.apps.googleusercontent.com",
 				fetch_basic_profile: true,
 				scope: "profile email"
 			});
 
 			self.googleAttachSignin(document.getElementById('btn-google-signin2-header-right'));
 			if(document.getElementById('btn-google-signin3-header-right')){
 				self.googleAttachSignin(document.getElementById('btn-google-signin3-header-right'));
 			}
 
 			// Sign the user in, and then retrieve their ID.
 			// auth2.signIn().then(function() {
 			// console.log(auth2.currentUser.get().getId());
 			// });
 		});
 		// gapi.signin2.render('btn-google-signin2-header-right', {
 		// 	'scope': 'profile email',
 		// 	'width': 50,
 		// 	'height': 50,
 		// 	'longtitle': false,
 		// 	'theme': 'dark',
 		// 	'onsuccess': onGoogleSignIn,
 		// 	'onfailure': onGoogleFailure
 		// });
 	};
 
 	self.googleAttachSignin = function(element) {
 		google_auth2.attachClickHandler(element, {}, self.onGoogleSignIn, self.onGoogleFailure);
 	};
 
 	self.onGoogleSignIn = function(googleUser) {
 		// Useful data for your client-side scripts:
 		// var profile = googleUser.getBasicProfile();
 		// console.log("ID: " + profile.getId()); // Don't send this directly to your server!
 		// console.log('Full Name: ' + profile.getName());
 		// console.log('Given Name: ' + profile.getGivenName());
 		// console.log('Family Name: ' + profile.getFamilyName());
 		// console.log("Image URL: " + profile.getImageUrl());
 		// console.log("Email: " + profile.getEmail());
 		self.googleSignOnWithBackend(googleUser);
 	};
 
 	self.onGoogleFailure = function(error){
 		//console.log('onFailure:');
 		//console.log(arguments);
 		//alert(JSON.stringify(error, undefined, 2));
 	};
 
 	self.googleSignOnWithBackend = function(user){
 		var user = gapi.auth2.getAuthInstance().currentUser.get();
 		var profile = user.getBasicProfile();
 		var id_token = user.getAuthResponse().id_token;
 
 		if(id_token === undefined) return;
 
 		// $.post('plugin/?id=google:verify&action=tryLogin', {id_token: id_token}, function(data){
 		// 	console.log(data);
 		// }, 'json');
 		var form = $('<form action="plugin/?id=google:verify&action=tryLogin&referer=" method="post"></form>');
 		form.append('<input type="hidden" name="id_token" value="">');
 		form.append('<input type="hidden" name="regsubmit" value="yes">');

 	var self = this;
 	var google_auth2;
 
 	self.onLoadGAPI = function(){
 		gapi.load('auth2', function() {
 			google_auth2 = gapi.auth2.init({

 				fetch_basic_profile: true,
 				scope: "profile email"
 			});
 
 			self.googleAttachSignin(document.getElementById('btn-google-signin2-header-right'));
 			if(document.getElementById('btn-google-signin3-header-right')){
 				self.googleAttachSignin(document.getElementById('btn-google-signin3-header-right'));
 			}
 
 			// Sign the user in, and then retrieve their ID.
 			// auth2.signIn().then(function() {
 			// console.log(auth2.currentUser.get().getId());
 			// });
 		});
 		// gapi.signin2.render('btn-google-signin2-header-right', {
 		// 	'scope': 'profile email',
 		// 	'width': 50,
 		// 	'height': 50,
 		// 	'longtitle': false,
 		// 	'theme': 'dark',
 		// 	'onsuccess': onGoogleSignIn,
 		// 	'onfailure': onGoogleFailure
 		// });
 	};
 
 	self.googleAttachSignin = function(element) {
 		google_auth2.attachClickHandler(element, {}, self.onGoogleSignIn, self.onGoogleFailure);
 	};
 
 	self.onGoogleSignIn = function(googleUser) {
 		// Useful data for your client-side scripts:
 		// var profile = googleUser.getBasicProfile();
 		// console.log("ID: " + profile.getId()); // Don't send this directly to your server!
 		// console.log('Full Name: ' + profile.getName());
 		// console.log('Given Name: ' + profile.getGivenName());
 		// console.log('Family Name: ' + profile.getFamilyName());
 		// console.log("Image URL: " + profile.getImageUrl());
 		// console.log("Email: " + profile.getEmail());
 		self.googleSignOnWithBackend(googleUser);
 	};
 
 	self.onGoogleFailure = function(error){
 		//console.log('onFailure:');
 		//console.log(arguments);
 		//alert(JSON.stringify(error, undefined, 2));
 	};
 
 	self.googleSignOnWithBackend = function(user){
 		var user = gapi.auth2.getAuthInstance().currentUser.get();
 		var profile = user.getBasicProfile();
 		var id_token = user.getAuthResponse().id_token;
 
 		if(id_token === undefined) return;
 
 		// $.post('plugin/?id=google:verify&action=tryLogin', {id_token: id_token}, function(data){
 		// 	console.log(data);
 		// }, 'json');
 		var form = $('<form action="plugin/?id=google:verify&action=tryLogin&referer=" method="post"></form>');
 		form.append('<input type="hidden" name="id_token" value="">');
 		form.append('<input type="hidden" name="regsubmit" value="yes">');
 		form.append('<input type="hidden" name="formhash" value="07b03726">');
 		form.append('<input type="hidden" name="referer" id="referer" value="" />');
 		form.find('input[name="id_token"]').val(id_token);
 		jQuery.post('plugin/?id=google:verify&action=tryLogin&referer=',jQuery(form[0]).serialize(),function(data){
 			window.location.href='https://www.jkforum.net/member.php?mod=logging&action=login&mobile=yes&g=return';
 		});
 	};
 
 	self.on = function(eventName, func){
 		self[eventName] && self[eventName].push(func);
 	};
 	self.dispatchEvent = function(eventName, event, context){
 		for(var i in self[eventName]){
 			self[eventName][i].call(context, event);
 		}
 	};
 })).$new(jQuery));
 
 function JK_GAPI_LOADED(){
 	jkfjs.google.onLoadGAPI.apply(this, arguments);
 }

     list-style: none;
     height: 10000px;
     top: 0;
     left: 0;
     position: absolute;
 }
 
 /*
     These are the items
 */
 .cbox_carousel li.smdiv_a {
 height:140px;
 margin-bottom: 10px;
 margin-right:0;
 }
 .cbox_carousel li.smdiv_a a, .cbox_carousel li.smdiv_a a:hover {color:#fff;}
 
 .cbox_carousel li.smdiv_a,
 .cbox_carousel li.smdiv_a span{
 width:100%;
 }
 
 .cbox_carousel .prev, .cbox_carousel .next{ color:#ccc; cursor:pointer;}
 
 .cbox_carousel > .disabled i {
 cursor: initial;
 opacity: 0.2;
 -moz-opacity: 0.2;
 filter:alpha(opacity=20);
 }

    jkfjs.install('google', (new JKDefineClass('GooglePlugin', function($){
 	var self = this;
 	var google_auth2;
 
 	self.onLoadGAPI = function(){
 		gapi.load('auth2', function() {
 			google_auth2 = gapi.auth2.init({
 				client_id: "822113201045-d7i1ef7c3djluutebumk2l4n8aa6if3s.apps.googleusercontent.com",
 				fetch_basic_profile: true,
 				scope: "profile email"
 			});
 
 			self.googleAttachSignin(document.getElementById('btn-google-signin2-header-right'));
 			if(document.getElementById('btn-google-signin3-header-right')){
 				self.googleAttachSignin(document.getElementById('btn-google-signin3-header-right'));
 			}
 
 			// Sign the user in, and then retrieve their ID.
 			// auth2.signIn().then(function() {
 			// console.log(auth2.currentUser.get().getId());
 			// });
 		});
 		// gapi.signin2.render('btn-google-signin2-header-right', {
 		// 	'scope': 'profile email',
 		// 	'width': 50,
 		// 	'height': 50,
 		// 	'longtitle': false,
 		// 	'theme': 'dark',
 		// 	'onsuccess': onGoogleSignIn,
 		// 	'onfailure': onGoogleFailure
 		// });
 	};
 
 	self.googleAttachSignin = function(element) {
 		google_auth2.attachClickHandler(element, {}, self.onGoogleSignIn, self.onGoogleFailure);
 	};
 
 	self.onGoogleSignIn = function(googleUser) {
 		// Useful data for your client-side scripts:
 		// var profile = googleUser.getBasicProfile();
 		// console.log("ID: " + profile.getId()); // Don't send this directly to your server!
 		// console.log('Full Name: ' + profile.getName());
 		// console.log('Given Name: ' + profile.getGivenName());
 		// console.log('Family Name: ' + profile.getFamilyName());
 		// console.log("Image URL: " + profile.getImageUrl());
 		// console.log("Email: " + profile.getEmail());
 		self.googleSignOnWithBackend(googleUser);
 	};
 
 	self.onGoogleFailure = function(error){
 		//console.log('onFailure:');
 		//console.log(arguments);
 		//alert(JSON.stringify(error, undefined, 2));
 	};
 
 	self.googleSignOnWithBackend = function(user){
 		var user = gapi.auth2.getAuthInstance().currentUser.get();
 		var profile = user.getBasicProfile();
 		var id_token = user.getAuthResponse().id_token;
 
 		if(id_token === undefined) return;
 
 		// $.post('plugin/?id=google:verify&action=tryLogin', {id_token: id_token}, function(data){
 		// 	console.log(data);
 		// }, 'json');
 		var form = $('<form action="plugin/?id=google:verify&action=tryLogin&referer=" method="post"></form>');
 		form.append('<input type="hidden" name="id_token" value="">');
 		form.append('<input type="hidden" name="regsubmit" value="yes">');
 		form.append('<input type="hidden" name="formhash" value="07b03726">');
 		form.append('<input type="hidden" name="referer" id="referer" value="" />');
 		form.find('input[name="id_token"]').val(id_token);
 		jQuery.post('plugin/?id=google:verify&action=tryLogin&referer=',jQuery(form[0]).serialize(),function(data){
 			window.location.href='https://www.jkforum.net/member.php?mod=logging&action=login&mobile=yes&g=return';
 		});
 	};
 
 	self.on = function(eventName, func){
 		self[eventName] && self[eventName].push(func);
 	};
 	self.dispatchEvent = function(eventName, event, context){
 		for(var i in self[eventName]){
 			self[eventName][i].call(context, event);
 		}
 	};
 })).$new(jQuery));
 
 function JK_GAPI_LOADED(){
 	jkfjs.google.onLoadGAPI.apply(this, arguments);
 }
